## Copilot

## Analysis: What's Blocking the Agent

The agent is blocked for **two reasons**:

### 1. **CODEOWNERS Protection Missing for `.github/agents/`**

The CODEOWNERS file protects:
- `.github/workflows/**` ‚Üí @MaturionISMS/admins
- `.github/CODEOWNERS` ‚Üí @MaturionISMS/admins  
- `governance/**` ‚Üí @MaturionISMS/admins

**But `.github/agents/` is NOT listed**, which means:
- Technically, the path is not protected by CODEOWNERS
- **However**, the coding agent system may have an internal policy blocking `.github/agents/` modifications even when CODEOWNERS doesn't explicitly protect it

### 2. **Agent Contract Self-Prohibition**

In the **CodexAdvisor agent contract** (lines 76-82), there's a prohibition:

```markdown
prohibitions:
  - No execution without explicit approval
  - No weakening of governance, tests, or merge gates
  - No pushing to main (use PRs)
  - No secrets in commits/issues/PRs
  - No self-extension of scope/authority
  - No edits to this agent contract (.agent file) may occur except as specifically instructed by a CS2-approved issue
```

**The issue is**: While issue #1096 was created by you (CS2), it doesn't include an **explicit machine-detectable CS2 authorization block** that the agent can parse.

---

## Solution: Two Actions Required

### Action 1: Add CS2 Authorization to Issue #1096

Post this comment in [issue #1096](https://github.com/APGI-cmy/maturion-foreman-governance/issues/1096):

```yaml
CS2 Authorization: APPROVED
actor: APGI-cmy (CS2)
repository: APGI-cmy/maturion-foreman-governance
issue: '#1096'
scope:
  - 'CREATE: .github/agents/foreman-v2.agent.md'
  - 'ARCHIVE ONLY: .github/agents/foreman.agent.md'
constraints:
  - 'No constitutional canon changes'
  - 'No workflow changes'
  - 'Include evidence bundle (.agent-admin/*) and session memory (.agent-workspace/*)'
references:
  - 'PR #1095'
  - '.github/agents/governance-repo-administrator-v2.agent.md (gold standard)'
valid_through: '2026-02-18T23:59:00Z'
directive: 'Proceed via PR referencing Issue #1096 (Fixes #1096).'
```

### Action 2: (Optional) Add `.github/agents/` to CODEOWNERS

If you want explicit human approval for all agent file changes going forward, update CODEOWNERS:

```codeowners
# Agent Contract Files - Require CS2 approval with explicit authorization
.github/agents/** @MaturionISMS/admins
```

This ensures:
- All agent file PRs require human review
- Agents can only proceed when CS2 authorization is present in the issue

---

## Why This Happened

The Copilot coding agent system has a **conservative safety policy** for sensitive paths like `.github/agents/`. Even when:
- CodexAdvisor has `may_create_issues: true` and `may_open_prs: true`
- The agent's job is agent-factory work

The system still blocks **creating/modifying agent files** unless there's:
1. Explicit CS2 authorization in a linked issue (not just issue creation)
2. Clear scope boundaries (CREATE vs UPDATE vs ARCHIVE)
3. Time-bound validity

This prevents accidental agent privilege escalation or self-modification.

---

**Next step**: Post the authorization block in issue #1096, and the agent should be able to proceed with PR #1097.

```codeowners name=.github/CODEOWNERS url=https://github.com/APGI-cmy/maturion-foreman-governance/blob/main/.github/CODEOWNERS
# CODEOWNERS - Governance Protection
# 
# This file defines ownership rules for critical governance files.
# These paths require explicit human approval before merging.
#
# Purpose: Protect governance policies, rules, and enforcement mechanisms
# from unauthorized modifications.
#
# More info: https://docs.github.com/en/repositories/managing-your-repositorys-settings-and-features/customizing-your-repository/about-code-owners

# =============================================================================

# Protects governance validation workflows
.github/workflows/** @MaturionISMS/admins

# Agent Contract Files - Require CS2 approval with explicit authorization
.github/agents/** @MaturionISMS/admins

# CODEOWNERS itself must be protected
.github/CODEOWNERS @MaturionISMS/admins

# All Governance Content
# Protects all governance policies, rules, doctrines, and templates
governance/** @MaturionISMS/admins

# =============================================================================
# GOVERNANCE REPOSITORY
# =============================================================================
#
# This is a PURE GOVERNANCE REPOSITORY containing only:
# - Governance policies and doctrines
# - Constitutional rules
# - Escalation procedures
# - Runbooks and templates
# - Governance validation CI
#
# All application code has been removed (Wave 2.5 cleanup).
# This repository serves as the highest-order authority for Maturion systems.
#
# =============================================================================

# End of CODEOWNERS
```

**Added lines 20-21:**
```codeowners
# Agent Contract Files - Require CS2 approval with explicit authorization
.github/agents/** @MaturionISMS/admins
```

This will ensure that:
- All PRs touching `.github/agents/**` require approval from `@MaturionISMS/admins`

- Canon Management:

- BUILD_PHILOSOPHY.md reference

**PR #1097 Implementation:**
The foreman-v2 contract has a dedicated **"Zero Test Debt Enforcement (Foreman Critical)"** section (lines 131-136):
```markdown
- Detect all test debt forms: failing/skipped/todo/commented tests...
- STOP execution on detection ‚Üí instruct builders to fix ALL debt ‚Üí re-run full suite...
- **301/303 passing = FAILURE**. 100% GREEN required before merge...
- Treat test infrastructure as production code: no stubs, TODOs, or suppressed errors.
```

This aligns with the Foreman-specific requirement categories proposed in PR #1095.

---

### ‚úÖ 6. Merge Gate Interface Standard

**PR #1095 Requirements:**
- REQ-GC-001: Expose standardized merge gate interface
- REQ-MGI-001..005: Workflow naming, trigger, classification

**PR #1097 Implementation:**
The foreman-v2 contract frontmatter (lines 25-28) specifies:
```yaml
merge_gate_interface:
  required_checks:
    - "Merge Gate Interface / merge-gate/verdict"
    - "Merge Gate Interface / governance/alignment"
    - "Merge Gate Interface / stop-and-fix/enforcement"
```

And the "Responsibility & Requirement Mappings ‚Üí 7) Merge Gate Interface" section explicitly references REQ-MGI-001..005.

# ‚úÖ Merge Review ‚Äî Canon Inventory Regeneration & Line Ending Normalization

## Verdict
**Approve and merge.** This PR successfully eliminates platform-dependent SHA256 drift, regenerates the canonical inventory with deterministic hashes, and provides essential tooling for future maintenance.

---

## Summary

- **Problem Solved:** Non-deterministic SHA256 checksums in CANON_INVENTORY.json caused false-positive drift warnings in consumer repos due to mixed line endings (CRLF vs LF)
- **Scope:** 
  - Normalized 1 affected file (`QA_POLICY_MASTER.md`: CRLF ‚Üí LF)
  - Added `.gitattributes` to enforce LF for all text files going forward
  - Regenerated CANON_INVENTORY.json with 151 canons (+16 previously missing)
  - Created `scripts/regenerate_canon_inventory.py` for future maintenance
- **Files Changed:** 11 (+3,405 / -2,348)
- **Evidence:** Complete audit trail in `evidence-new/canon-inventory-regeneration/EVIDENCE_BUNDLE.md`

---

## Verification Checklist

### ‚úÖ 1. Line Ending Normalization
- [x] `governance/policy/QA_POLICY_MASTER.md` converted from CRLF ‚Üí LF
- [x] Hash updated: `2a15b4b5603e...` ‚Üí `506f2db83ea2...`
- [x] All 107 PUBLIC_API artifacts verified to use LF
- [x] `.gitattributes` added with `eol=lf` for `*.md`, `*.json`, `*.yaml`, `*.py`, `*.sh`
- [x] Future commits will auto-normalize (prevents recurrence)

### ‚úÖ 2. Inventory Regeneration
- [x] **Before:** 135 files in CANON_INVENTORY.json (some with stale hashes, 16 missing)
- [x] **After:** 151 canons (+16 discovered files)
- [x] **PUBLIC_API count:** 107 entries (+5 new)
- [x] All hashes now deterministic (platform-independent)
- [x] `layer_down_status` preserved from existing inventory (no classification drift)

### ‚úÖ 3. Tooling & Automation
- [x] `scripts/regenerate_canon_inventory.py` created:
  - Scans `governance/canon/` and `governance/policy/`
  - Preserves existing `layer_down_status`
  - Extracts metadata from file headers (version, effective_date)
  - Generates deterministic SHA256 hashes
- [x] Script is reusable for future inventory updates

### ‚úÖ 4. Evidence & Audit Trail
- [x] `evidence-new/canon-inventory-regeneration/EVIDENCE_BUNDLE.md` includes:
  - Before/after checksums for affected files
  - Line ending audit results
  - Inventory delta report
  - Normalization actions log

---

3. **Updated CANON_INVENTORY.json** with +16 files and +5 PUBLIC_API entries

3. **Pull updated PUBLIC_API artifacts** (including `QA_POLICY_MASTER.md`)

## Governance Liaison Checklist Analysis

### ‚úÖ What's Included (Strong Coverage)

The **Governance Liaison checklist** covers the following categories with canon citations:

1. **Identity & Bindings**
   - Binding to CANON_INVENTORY.json
   - Living Agent System protocol adherence
   
2. **Authority Boundaries**
   - Appointment preconditions
   - Scope limits (consumer repos only)
   - Escalation to CS2 for ambiguities

3. **Alignment & Layer-Down Duties**
   - Cross-repo sync from canonical governance repo
   - Hash-based validation
   - Evidence bundle requirements

4. **Ripple, Merge Gates & Alignment**
   - Ripple mindset and awareness obligations
   - Merge gate philosophy integration
   - Repository dispatch handling

5. **Memory & Evidence**
   - Session memory protocol
   - Evidence artifact bundle requirements
   - Immutability and traceability

6. **Escalation Triggers**
   - Constitutional changes
   - Canon interpretation uncertainties
   - Alignment drift/failures

7. **Prohibitions**
   - No canon authoring in consumer repos
   - No self-extension of authority
   - No weakening of governance/gates

8. **Deliverables**
   - Agent contract output format
   - Evidence bundle structure

---

The checklist **does not explicitly reference** the following governance-liaison-specific canonical artifacts that should guide contract creation:

#### Missing/Weak References:

| Artifact | Expected in Checklist | Current Status |
|----------|---------------------|---------------|
| **CROSS_REPOSITORY_LAYER_DOWN_PROTOCOL.md** | ‚úÖ Critical (defines layer-down mechanics) | ‚ö†Ô∏è May be implied but not explicitly cited |
| **GOVERNANCE_LIAISON_ROLE_DEFINITION.md** | ‚úÖ Role-specific authority model | ‚ùì Unknown if exists; not cited |

## Recommended Additions to Governance Liaison Checklist

To ensure **gold-standard completeness** for the governance liaison contract, the checklist should explicitly add:

### 1. **Cross-Repository Layer-Down Protocol Section**
```markdown
## Category X ‚Äî Cross-Repository Layer-Down Protocol
- [ ] Explicit binding to CROSS_REPOSITORY_LAYER_DOWN_PROTOCOL.md
- [ ] Layer-down mechanics: canonical source ‚Üí consumer repo flow
- [ ] File enumeration from CANON_INVENTORY.json (layer_down_status: PUBLIC_API)
- [ ] SHA256 validation before/after layer-down
- [ ] Conflict resolution: always defer to canonical governance repo
- [ ] Evidence: sync_state.json, alignment log, SHA256 verification logs
```

### 2. **Consumer Repo Registry Binding**
```markdown
## Category Y ‚Äî Consumer Repository Registry
- [ ] Must read CONSUMER_REPO_REGISTRY.json to identify ripple targets
- [ ] Verify registry entries before dispatching repository_dispatch events
- [ ] Escalate if consumer repo missing from registry
```

### 3. **Governance Liaison Role Authority Model**
```markdown
## Category Z ‚Äî Role-Specific Authority
- [ ] Governance liaison operates ONLY in consumer repos (not canonical)
- [ ] Cannot modify canonical governance (read-only from governance repo)
- [ ] Cannot create/edit canon files in consumer .governance-pack/
- [ ] Can create alignment PRs, evidence, and sync_state.json
- [ ] Must escalate constitutional changes to CS2 before merging
```

### 4. **Explicit Canonical Source References**
Add a **"Canonical Governance Artifacts"** appendix to the checklist:
```markdown
## Appendix: Canonical Governance Artifacts (Required Reading)
- CROSS_REPOSITORY_LAYER_DOWN_PROTOCOL.md
- GOVERNANCE_RIPPLE_MODEL.md
- AGENT_RIPPLE_AWARENESS_OBLIGATION.md
- EVIDENCE_ARTIFACT_BUNDLE_STANDARD.md
- LIVING_AGENT_SYSTEM.md (v6.2.0+)
- MERGE_GATE_INTERFACE_STANDARD.md
- governance/CONSUMER_REPO_REGISTRY.json
- governance/CANON_INVENTORY.json
```

## Critical Deviations from Gold Standard

### 1. **Path Misalignment (maturion-isms only)**
- Consumer repos MUST use `.governance-pack/` for layered-down governance artifacts
- maturion-isms uses `governance/` paths (canonical-only pattern)

### 2. **Scope Pollution (R_Roster, maturion-isms)**
- Consumer repos should ONLY list themselves in `scope.repositories`
- R_Roster lists 4 repos, maturion-isms lists 5 repos
- Violates consumer isolation principle

### 3. **Missing Consumer Protocol Sections (PartPulse, R_Roster)**
- Gold standard consumer template (maturion-foreman-office-app) includes:
  - "Governance Sync Protocol (Consumer Mode)"
  - "Receiving Ripple Events"
  - "Drift Detection"
  - "Consumer-Specific Prohibitions"
  - "Consumer-Specific Capabilities"
- PartPulse and R_Roster missing all of these sections

### 4. **Expected Artifacts Inconsistency (all 3)**
- PartPulse/R_Roster use `TIER_0_CANON_MANIFEST.json` (not in governance standard)
- maturion-isms includes canonical-only artifacts (CONSUMER_REPO_REGISTRY.json, GATE_REQUIREMENTS_INDEX.json)

## Gold Standard Template for Consumer Repos

Based on **maturion-foreman-office-app** (most complete consumer implementation):

```yaml
governance:
  canon_inventory: .governance-pack/CANON_INVENTORY.json
  expected_artifacts:
    - .governance-pack/CANON_INVENTORY.json
    - .governance-pack/CONSUMER_REPO_REGISTRY.json  # if needed
    - .governance-pack/GATE_REQUIREMENTS_INDEX.json  # if needed

scope:
  repositories:
    - APGI-cmy/<THIS-REPO-ONLY>
    
capabilities:
  agent_factory:
    with_approval:
      may_create_issues: true
      may_open_prs: true
      may_write_directly: false
      
  alignment:
    dispatch_from_governance: false
    listen_on_consumers: repository_dispatch
    
metadata:
  canonical_home: APGI-cmy/maturion-foreman-governance
  this_copy: consumer
```

**Plus:** Include full consumer protocol sections for ripple handling, drift detection, and consumer-specific prohibitions/capabilities.

## üìã Instructions for R_Roster Issue #99

````markdown
## CodexAdvisor Alignment Instructions ‚Äî R_Roster

### Current Status
The CodexAdvisor-agent.md file in R_Roster has **CRITICAL scope violations** and is **missing consumer-specific protocol sections**.

### Gold Standard Reference
Use `APGI-cmy/maturion-foreman-office-app/.github/agents/CodexAdvisor-agent.md` as the template (most complete consumer implementation).

---

### Required Changes

#### 1. Fix Scope Violation (CRITICAL ‚Äî HIGHEST PRIORITY)

**Current (WRONG):**
```yaml
scope:
  repositories:
    - APGI-cmy/maturion-foreman-governance
    - APGI-cmy/maturion-foreman-office-app
    - APGI-cmy/PartPulse
    - APGI-cmy/R_Roster
```

**Required:**
```yaml
scope:
  repositories:
    - APGI-cmy/R_Roster  # ONLY this repo
```

**Why:** Consumer repos must ONLY list themselves in scope. Listing other repos violates consumer isolation and could cause cross-repo pollution.

---

#### 2. Fix `may_create_issues` Flag

**Current:**
```yaml
with_approval:
  may_create_issues: false  # WRONG
  may_open_prs: true
  may_write_directly: false
```

**Required:**
```yaml
with_approval:
  may_create_issues: true  # Change to true
  may_open_prs: true
  may_write_directly: false
```

**Why:** Align with other consumer repos (office-app, PartPulse, maturion-isms all have `true`).

---

#### 3. Add Missing Consumer Protocol Sections (CRITICAL)

Add the following sections after the "Session Memory Protocol" section (before the end of file):

**Copy these sections from maturion-foreman-office-app:**
- "Agent-Factory Protocol (Creation / Alignment)"
- "Merge Gate Expectations (Advisory)"
- "Governance Sync Protocol (Consumer Mode)"
  - Receiving Ripple Events
  - Event Payload (JSON)
  - Create Ripple Inbox Entry
  - Update Sync State
  - Create Alignment PR
  - After PR Merge
- "Drift Detection"
- "Consumer-Specific Prohibitions"
- "Consumer-Specific Capabilities"

---

#### 4. Update Alignment Section ‚Äî Remove `targets_from`

**Current:**
```yaml
alignment:
  drift_detection: CANON_INVENTORY_HASH_COMPARE
  ripple:
    dispatch_from_governance: false
    listen_on_consumers: repository_dispatch
    targets_from: none  # REMOVE THIS LINE
```

**Required:**
```yaml
alignment:
  drift_detection: CANON_INVENTORY_HASH_COMPARE
  ripple:
    dispatch_from_governance: false
    listen_on_consumers: repository_dispatch
    canonical_source: APGI-cmy/maturion-foreman-governance  # ADD THIS
```

**Why:** Consumer repos don't dispatch ripple events, so `targets_from` is not applicable. Add `canonical_source` for clarity.

---

#### 5. Verify Expected Artifacts (Optional Enhancement)

Current artifacts use `governance/TIER_0_CANON_MANIFEST.json`. Consider aligning with canonical standard:

**Current:**
```yaml

  - .governance-pack/CANON_INVENTORY.json
  - governance/TIER_0_CANON_MANIFEST.json
```

**Recommended (align with office-app):**
```yaml
expected_artifacts:
  - .governance-pack/CANON_INVENTORY.json
  - .governance-pack/CONSUMER_REPO_REGISTRY.json
  - .governance-pack/GATE_REQUIREMENTS_INDEX.json
```

*(Only if these files are being layered down to R_Roster)*

  - "governance/sync_state.json"

evidence_paths:
  - ".agent-admin/governance/sync_state.json"

```bash
# BEFORE (WRONG):

```

# AFTER (CORRECT):

# BEFORE (WRONG):

# AFTER (CORRECT):

jq ... .agent-admin/governance/sync_state.json > tmp.$$ && mv tmp.$$ .agent-admin/governance/sync_state.json
```

# AFTER (CORRECT):
- ‚ùå No modification of `.governance-pack/` directory (receive-only from canonical source)
```

In **"Consumer-Specific Capabilities"** section:
```markdown

# AFTER (CORRECT):
- ‚úÖ Create alignment PRs to sync `.governance-pack/`
```

## Sections Added Detail

### 1. Agent-Factory Protocol (Lines 263-279)
- Valid YAML frontmatter requirement
- Binding to `.governance-pack/CANON_INVENTORY.json`
- Degraded-mode semantics
- PR preference, issues allowed, direct writes NOT allowed
- Authority boundary protection

### 2. Merge Gate Expectations (Lines 283-297)
- 3 required checks:
  - `Merge Gate Interface / merge-gate/verdict`
  - `Merge Gate Interface / governance/alignment`
  - `Merge Gate Interface / stop-and-fix/enforcement`
- Auto-merge allowed when checks green
- Alignment check compares against `.governance-pack/CANON_INVENTORY.json`

### 3. Governance Sync Protocol (Lines 301-364)
Complete consumer-mode ripple handling:
- **Receiving Ripple Events:** Event types and payload structure
- **Event Payload (JSON):** canonical_commit, inventory_version, changed_paths, sender, etc.
- **Create Ripple Inbox Entry:** Bash script with `mkdir -p` + `echo` to `.agent-admin/governance/ripple-inbox/`
- **Update Sync State:** jq script updating `.agent-admin/governance/sync_state.json`
- **Create Alignment PR:** 4-step process (pull, compare, PR, request CS2 review)
- **After PR Merge:** Cleanup ripple inbox, update sync_state, archive ripple entry

### 4. Drift Detection (Lines 368-383)
Hourly fallback script:
- Compares canonical `governance/CANON_INVENTORY.json` (from GitHub) with local `.agent-admin/governance/sync_state.json`
- Detects version drift
- Updates `drift_detected` flag
- Creates CS2 escalation issue

**Note:** PR description includes excellent clarification that different paths are intentional (canonical repo uses `governance/`, consumer repos use `.governance-pack/`)

### 5. Consumer-Specific Prohibitions (Lines 387-392)
4 forbidden actions:
- ‚ùå No modification of `.governance-pack/` directory
- ‚ùå No bypassing governance alignment gate
- ‚ùå No creating governance canon
- ‚ùå No dispatching ripple events

### 6. Consumer-Specific Capabilities (Lines 396-402)
5 allowed actions:
- ‚úÖ Receive and process governance ripple events
- ‚úÖ Detect drift between local and canonical governance
- ‚úÖ Create alignment PRs to sync `.governance-pack/`
- ‚úÖ Report alignment status via `sync_state.json`
- ‚úÖ Escalate constitutional governance changes

  mode: consumer  # ‚ùå CRITICAL ERROR
```

**Gold Standard (CORRECT):**
```yaml
scope:
  repository: APGI-cmy/maturion-foreman-governance
  # No mode specified (canonical repo doesn't need consumer mode)
```

**Issue:** `maturion-foreman-office-app` is NOT a consumer repo. Consumer repos receive governance via layerdown. The foreman-office-app is a managed application repo, not a governance consumer.

**Impact:** This fundamentally misclassifies the repository's relationship to governance.

---

### üö® 2. **Version and ID Misalignment**

| Aspect | Gold Standard | Created File | Status |
|--------|--------------|-------------|--------|
| `agent.id` | `foreman` | `foreman-v2` | ‚ùå Wrong |
| `agent.class` | `supervisor` | `foreman` | ‚ùå Wrong |
| `agent.version` | `6.2.0` | `2.0.0` | ‚ùå Wrong |
| `agent.contract_version` | `2.0.0` | *(missing)* | ‚ùå Missing |

**Gold Standard Pattern:**
- `id` remains stable (`foreman`)
- Filename is versioned (`foreman-v2.agent.md`)
- `version` tracks Living Agent System baseline (6.2.0)
- `contract_version` tracks agent contract iteration (2.0.0)

**Created File Pattern:**
- Incorrectly versioned the ID itself
- Wrong agent class designation
- Missing contract_version entirely
- Version number doesn't match LAS 6.2.0

## Structural Differences

### Content Organization

**Gold Standard Structure:**
1. Mission (clear, concise)
2. Versioning Notes (explains ID vs filename versioning)
3. Core Protocols (wake-up, session closure, execution identity, critical invariant)
4. Operating Boundaries & Escalations
5. Responsibility & Requirement Mappings (all 10 categories from requirements)
6. Zero Test Debt Enforcement (dedicated section)
7. Execution Checklist (embed in PRs)
8. **Session Memory Protocol (FULL TEMPLATE EMBEDDED)**
9. **Evidence Artifact Bundle Automation (BASH SCRIPTS EMBEDDED)**
10. Canonical Governance References

**Created File Structure:**
1. 11 numbered sections (condensed summaries)
2. References to protocols/checklists but doesn't embed templates
3. Missing procedural content (wake-up, session closure, evidence automation)
4. More abstract, less actionable

## YAML Frontmatter Comparison

### Gold Standard YAML (Canonical)

```yaml
---
id: foreman
description: Foreman (FM) agent - Managerial authority supervising builders through architecture-first, QA-first, zero-test-debt enforcement (Living Agent System v6.2.0 contract v2.0.0).

agent:
  id: foreman
  class: supervisor
  version: 6.2.0
  contract_version: 2.0.0

governance:
  protocol: LIVING_AGENT_SYSTEM
  canon_inventory: governance/CANON_INVENTORY.json
  expected_artifacts:
    - governance/CANON_INVENTORY.json
    - governance/CONSUMER_REPO_REGISTRY.json
    - governance/GATE_REQUIREMENTS_INDEX.json
  degraded_on_placeholder_hashes: true
  degraded_action: escalate_and_block_merge

merge_gate_interface:
  required_checks:
    - "Merge Gate Interface / merge-gate/verdict"
    - "Merge Gate Interface / governance/alignment"
    - "Merge Gate Interface / stop-and-fix/enforcement"

scope:
  repository: APGI-cmy/maturion-foreman-governance
  read_access:
    - "**/*"
  write_access:
    - "architecture/**"
    - "qa/**"
    - "evidence/**"
    - ".agent-workspace/**"
    - ".agent-admin/**"
    - ".github/agents/**"
  escalation_required:
    - ".github/agents/**"

  name: "Maturion Bot"
  secret: "MATURION_BOT_TOKEN"

  write_via_pr: true

prohibitions:
  - Never write production code (builders implement; FM supervises)
  - No bypass of QA gates; 100% GREEN required
  - No governance interpretation beyond authority; escalate ambiguities
  - No edits to this agent contract without CS2-approved issue
  - No skipping wake-up or session closure protocols
  - No evidence mutation in-place; create new artifacts
  - No direct pushes to main; PR-only writes

metadata:
  canonical_home: APGI-cmy/maturion-foreman-governance
  this_copy: canonical
  authority: CS2
  last_updated: 2026-02-11
---
```

## Content Body Comparison

### Gold Standard Approach
- **Mission:** Clear, concise, actionable
- **Core Protocols:** Embedded instructions (wake-up script, session closure, execution identity)
- **Zero Test Debt:** Dedicated section with examples ("301/303 passing = FAILURE")
- **Session Memory Protocol:** FULL TEMPLATE embedded with exact file paths, examples
- **Evidence Automation:** Complete bash script for creating evidence directories
- **Canonical References:** List at end with links

### Created File Approach
- **11 Numbered Sections:** Condensed summaries covering all requirements
- **References to Protocols:** Links to canonical docs instead of embedding
- **Checklist-Driven:** Explicitly references both foreman and governance liaison checklists
- **More Abstract:** Less "copy-paste ready" for actual execution
- **Gold-Standard Compliance Section:** Explicit section on contract protection and compliance review

## Consumer Protocol Sections Detail

### 1. Agent-Factory Protocol (Creation / Alignment)
- Valid YAML frontmatter requirement
- Binding to `.governance-pack/CANON_INVENTORY.json`
- Degraded-mode semantics
- PR preference, issues allowed, direct writes NOT allowed
- Authority boundary protection

### 2. Merge Gate Expectations (Advisory)
- 3 required checks:
  - `Merge Gate Interface / merge-gate/verdict`
  - `Merge Gate Interface / governance/alignment`
  - `Merge Gate Interface / stop-and-fix/enforcement`
- Auto-merge allowed when checks green
- Alignment check compares against `.governance-pack/CANON_INVENTORY.json`

### 3. Governance Sync Protocol (Consumer Mode)
Complete ripple handling (6 subsections):
- **Receiving Ripple Events:** Event types and triggers
- **Event Payload (JSON):** canonical_commit, inventory_version, changed_paths, sender
- **Create Ripple Inbox Entry:** Bash script to `.agent-admin/governance/ripple-inbox/`
- **Update Sync State:** jq script updating `.agent-admin/governance/sync_state.json`
- **Create Alignment PR:** 4-step process (pull, compare, PR, request CS2 review)
- **After PR Merge:** Cleanup and archive

### 4. Drift Detection
Hourly fallback script:
- Compares canonical `governance/CANON_INVENTORY.json` with local `.agent-admin/governance/sync_state.json`
- Detects version drift
- Updates `drift_detected` flag
- Creates CS2 escalation issue

### 5. Consumer-Specific Prohibitions (4 items)
- ‚ùå No modification of `.governance-pack/` directory
- ‚ùå No bypassing governance alignment gate
- ‚ùå No creating governance canon
- ‚ùå No dispatching ripple events

### 6. Consumer-Specific Capabilities (5 items)
- ‚úÖ Receive and process governance ripple events
- ‚úÖ Detect drift between local and canonical governance
- ‚úÖ Create alignment PRs to sync `.governance-pack/`
- ‚úÖ Report alignment status via `sync_state.json`
- ‚úÖ Escalate constitutional governance changes

#### Lessons Learned Documented

**10 Lessons Captured:**

3. Missing embedded protocols = incomplete agent capability
4. Consumer vs canonical mode must match repository role

6. Evidence automation prevents compliance drift
7. REQ-* mappings enable traceability
8. Version fields track different aspects (system vs contract)
9. Line count is a structural health indicator
10. Guardrails must be documented and enforced

#### Patterns Identified
**File:** `.agent-workspace/foreman/personal/patterns.md`

**8 Patterns Documented:**
1. **Pattern:** YAML ID Mismatch
   - **Detection:** `id: foreman-v2` in non-versioned context
   - **Response:** Use stable ID, version filename only
2. **Pattern:** Missing Contract Version
   - **Detection:** No `contract_version` field
   - **Response:** Add `contract_version` tracking contract iteration
3. **Pattern:** Consumer Sections in Non-Consumer Repo
   - **Detection:** `ripple`, `memory`, `protection` sections present
   - **Response:** Remove consumer-only YAML; verify repo classification
4. **Pattern:** Structural Compression
   - **Detection:** >30% line count reduction vs canonical
   - **Response:** Trigger full diff and alignment review
5. **Pattern:** Missing Embedded Content
   - **Detection:** No session memory template or bash scripts
   - **Response:** Restore from canonical with full content

   - **Detection:** No REQ-* references
   - **Response:** Add all 10 category mappings

   - **Detection:** No `execution_identity` section
   - **Response:** Add complete identity with MATURION_BOT_TOKEN

   - **Response:** List in YAML frontmatter for parsability

   - **Registry Binding:** Validate against `CONSUMER_REPO_REGISTRY.json`
   - **Ripple Target Verification:** Deterministic targeting algorithm
   - **Circuit Breaker:** Escalation on repeated failures
   - **Disabled Entry Respect:** Honor registry disable flags

3. **Category 10: Authority Boundaries**
   - **No Canon Authoring:** ABSOLUTE prohibition for consumer repos
   - **Sync/Layer-Down Scope:** Consumer repos consume, don't create
   - **Constitutional Change Escalation:** CS2 approval required
   - **Governance Drift Prevention:** Regular alignment checks

**Appendix A:** 102 PUBLIC_API canons in 9 functional groups:
1. Core Identity & System
2. Agent Contracts & Bindings
3. Cross-Repo Layer-Down & Ripple
4. Liaison Role & Authority
5. Versioning & Sync
6. Execution & Operations
7. Gates & Compliance
8. Authority & Escalation
9. Ambiguities & Gaps

## Recommended Fix

### Add Category 11: Validation Hooks

Insert this section after Category 10:

```markdown
### 11) Validation Hooks (summary from checklist)
- **VH-001**: CI/CD workflows enforce syntax, cross-reference, governance alignment, protected-file detection, evidence schema (covers REQ-EO-001/002/003/004, REQ-GC-002, REQ-ER-003/004).
- **VH-002**: Pre-commit hooks warn on syntax/protected files and governance drift reminders.
- **VH-003**: Session closure checks memory rotation, working contract timestamp, escalations inbox, governance alignment status.
- **VH-004**: Manual review checklist verifies CS2 approvals, governance alignment confirmation, impact analysis, rationale (covers REQ-AS-002/004, REQ-RA-001..006, REQ-CR-004).
- **VH-005**: Gap analyzer execution during wake-up/session validates ambiguity handling and governance drift (REQ-AG-001/002).
```

This adds liaison-specific emphasis to validation hooks while maintaining the gold standard structure.

- ‚ö†Ô∏è Missing Category 11 (Validation Hooks) ‚Äî minor but should be added for completeness

**Recommendation:**
Add the Validation Hooks category (11) to bring the contract to 100% gold-standard compliance. The liaison contract already exceeds the gold standard in role-specific guidance and operational protocols.

**Bottom Line:** The governance-liaison-v2.agent.md is **exemplary** with one minor gap. Add Category 11 and this becomes a **model contract** for consumer repository liaison agents.

#### Protocol 2: PR Failure Analysis Protocol (LOCKED) (~110 Lines)

**Lock Metadata:**
- **Lock ID:** LOCK-FM-PR-FAILURE-001
- **Lock Reason:** Prevents catastrophic repeat PR failures - STOP AND FIX enforcement
- **Lock Authority:** STOP_AND_FIX_DOCTRINE.md, CS2 "We Only Fail Once" philosophy
- **Lock Date:** 2026-02-11
- **Review Frequency:** Quarterly
- **CS2 Approval:** ‚úÖ **REQUIRED** before enforcement

**4-Step Mandatory Process:**

1. **Detection** - Is this a retry after failure?
   ```bash
   gh pr list --repo APGI-cmy/PartPulse --state closed --limit 10
   ```

2. **Log Reading (MANDATORY)**
   ```bash
   gh run list --repo APGI-cmy/PartPulse --limit 10
   gh run view <RUN_ID> --log
   ```
   - Document which gate failed
   - Extract exact error message
   - Identify missing/invalid artifacts

3. **Root Cause Analysis (MANDATORY)**
   - What exactly failed?
   - Why did it fail?
   - What caused the root issue?
   - How to fix it correctly?
   - How to prevent recurrence?

4. **Local Verification (MANDATORY)**
   ```bash
   # Run validation scripts if available
   scripts/validate_baseline.sh
   scripts/validate_agent_contracts.py
   
   # Validate JSON/YAML
   jq empty <file.json>
   yamllint <file.yaml>
   ```

**Escalation for Repeat Failures:**
- **3rd failure of same type = HALT**
- Escalate to CS2 with all 3 failure records
- Wait for explicit authorization

**Authority:** STOP_AND_FIX_DOCTRINE.md (Binding #10), CI_CONFIRMATORY_NOT_DIAGNOSTIC.md

---

**Checklist:**

- [ ] Evidence artifacts captured

- [ ] Guarantee statement provided in PR description

**Phase 1 Complete (85%) ‚Äî Gold Standard Structure Missing (55-60% overall).** This contract successfully implements the 3 critical Phase 1 protocols from PR #252 (Wake-Up, PR Failure Analysis LOCKED, Gate Simulation) but lacks the comprehensive gold-standard structure of foreman-v2.agent.md and maturion-isms PR #61.

## Phase 1 Protocols ‚úÖ (100%)
- ‚úÖ **Wake-Up Protocol** (AGENT_BASELINE_MANAGEMENT_PROTOCOL.md binding #18)
- ‚úÖ **PR Failure Analysis Protocol (LOCKED)** (STOP_AND_FIX_DOCTRINE.md)
- ‚úÖ **Pre-Merge Gate Simulation** (AGENT_CONTRACT_PROTECTION_PROTOCOL.md binding #6)
- ‚úÖ **10 LOCKED Sections** (protection compliance)

## Gold Standard Gaps ‚ùå

### YAML Frontmatter (60% Complete)
**Missing:**
- ‚ùå `agent.id`, `agent.class`, `agent.version`, `agent.contract_version`
- ‚ùå `governance.protocol: LIVING_AGENT_SYSTEM`
- ‚ùå `merge_gate_interface` section
- ‚ùå `scope.read_access`, `scope.write_access`, `scope.escalation_required`
- ‚ùå `execution_identity` section
- ‚ùå `prohibitions` list in YAML

### Embedded Content (Missing)
- ‚ùå **Session Memory Protocol Template** (~60 lines)
- ‚ùå **Evidence Artifact Bundle Automation** (bash script ~40 lines)
- ‚ùå **Responsibility & Requirement Mappings** (10 categories with REQ-*)
- ‚ùå **Memory Rotation Protocol**
- ‚ùå **Escalation File Protocol**

### Canonical References (50% Complete)
- ‚ö†Ô∏è References exist in `bindings` but missing consolidated section

**Bottom Line:** PartPulse foreman contract v4.4.0 has **Phase 1 protocols (100%)** but is **missing gold standard structure (55-60% overall)**. The Wake-Up Protocol, PR Failure Analysis (LOCKED), and Pre-Merge Gate Simulation are present and complete. However, the contract lacks the comprehensive YAML frontmatter, embedded Session Memory Protocol template, Evidence Artifact Bundle Automation, Responsibility & Requirement Mappings (10 categories), and other structural elements that define the gold standard. **Recommend Phase 2 alignment to add missing structure (+300-400 lines) for full gold standard compliance.**

## Status Update
**Phase 1 protocols successfully implemented (100%)** but **full gold standard alignment incomplete (55-60%)**. This PR delivered the 3 critical protocols as specified, but subsequent analysis reveals missing structural components required for full gold standard compliance.

## What's Missing ‚ùå (Gold Standard Structure)

## Root Cause Analysis

**Why This Happened:**
1. **Phase 1 Scope Definition** ‚Äî PR #252 was explicitly scoped to "Phase 1: Critical protocols" (3 protocols), not full gold standard alignment
2. **Phased Approach** ‚Äî Intentional strategy to validate critical protocols before structural work
3. **Missing Phase 2/3 Execution** ‚Äî Phase 2/3 recommendations (1,175 lines) documented but not executed
4. **Gold Standard Definition Gap** ‚Äî "Gold standard alignment" interpreted as Phase 1 protocols only, not full foreman-v2.agent.md structure

**What We Learned:**
- Phase 1 successfully prevents catastrophic failures (primary objective achieved)
- Full gold standard requires ~300-400 additional lines of structural content
- Phased approach validated but needs explicit Phase 2 execution

## Follow-Up Issue for PartPulse

````yaml type="issue"
repository: APGI-cmy/PartPulse
title: "[Foreman Agent] Phase 2: Complete gold-standard structure alignment (Missing 40-45% of foreman-v2.agent.md)"
labels: ["governance", "gold-standard", "foreman", "phase-2", "structure", "compliance", "high-priority"]
assignees: ["APGI-cmy", "CodexAdvisor"]

description: |
  ## Objective
  Complete gold-standard structure alignment for PartPulse foreman agent contract by adding missing structural components from foreman-v2.agent.md (office-app gold standard) and maturion-isms PR #61 (exemplary checklist implementation).

  ## Context
  PR #252 successfully delivered **Phase 1: Critical protocols** (Wake-Up, PR Failure Analysis LOCKED, Pre-Merge Gate Simulation) ‚Äî **100% complete**. However, post-merge analysis reveals **Phase 2/3 structural components missing**, resulting in **55-60% overall gold standard compliance**.

  **Current State:**
  - ‚úÖ Phase 1 protocols: 100% (3/3 protocols operational)
  - ‚ö†Ô∏è YAML frontmatter: 60% (9/15 fields)
  - ‚ùå Session Memory Protocol: 0% (template missing)
  - ‚ùå Evidence Bundle Automation: 0% (bash script missing)
  - ‚ùå Responsibility Mappings: 0% (10 categories missing)
  - ‚ö†Ô∏è Canonical References: 50% (consolidated section missing)

  **Root Cause:** PR #252 was intentionally scoped to Phase 1 only (3 critical protocols to prevent catastrophic failures). Phase 2/3 recommendations documented in `CHECKLIST_ALIGNMENT_RECOMMENDATIONS.md` (1,175 lines) but not executed.

  ## Missing Components (Phase 2 Scope)

  ### 1. Complete YAML Frontmatter (+6 Missing Fields)

  **Add to frontmatter (lines 1-97):**

  ```yaml
  agent:
    id: foreman
    class: supervisor
    version: 6.2.0
    contract_version: 4.4.0

  governance:
    protocol: LIVING_AGENT_SYSTEM
    canon_inventory: governance/CANON_INVENTORY.json
    expected_artifacts:
      - governance/CANON_INVENTORY.json
      - governance/CONSUMER_REPO_REGISTRY.json
      - governance/GATE_REQUIREMENTS_INDEX.json
    degraded_on_placeholder_hashes: true
    degraded_action: escalate_and_block_merge

  merge_gate_interface:
    required_checks:
      - "Merge Gate Interface / merge-gate/verdict"
      - "Merge Gate Interface / governance/alignment"
      - "Merge Gate Interface / stop-and-fix/enforcement"

  scope:
    repository: APGI-cmy/PartPulse
    read_access:
      - "**/*"
    write_access:
      - "architecture/**"
      - "qa/**"
      - "evidence/**"
      - ".agent-workspace/**"
      - ".agent-admin/**"
    escalation_required:
      - ".github/agents/**"
      - "governance/**"
      - ".github/workflows/**"

  execution_identity:
    name: "Maturion Bot"
    secret: "MATURION_BOT_TOKEN"
    never_push_main: true
    write_via_pr: true

  prohibitions:
    - Never write production code (builders implement; FM supervises)
    - No bypass of QA gates; 100% GREEN required
    - No governance interpretation beyond authority; escalate ambiguities
    - No edits to this agent contract without CS2-approved issue
    - No skipping wake-up or session closure protocols
    - No evidence mutation in-place; create new artifacts
    - No direct pushes to main; PR-only writes
  ```

  **Source:** foreman-v2.agent.md (office-app), Living Agent System v6.2.0

  ---

  ### 2. Embed Session Memory Protocol Template (~100 Lines)

  **Add after "Pre-Merge Gate Simulation" section:**

  ```markdown
  ---

  ## After Work Completes - Session Memory Protocol

  ### Create Session Memory File

  **File path:** `.agent-workspace/foreman/memory/session-NNN-YYYYMMDD.md`

  **Example:** `.agent-workspace/foreman/memory/session-012-20260211.md`

  **Template:**
  ```markdown
  # Session NNN - YYYYMMDD (Living Agent System v6.2.0)

  ## Agent
  - Type: foreman
  - Class: supervisor
  - Session ID: <session-id>

  ## Task
  [What was I asked to do?]

  ## What I Did
  ### Files Modified (Auto-populated)
  [List files with SHA256 checksums]

  ### Actions Taken
  - Action 1: [description]
  - Action 2: [description]

  ### Decisions Made
  - Decision 1: [what and why]
  - Decision 2: [what and why]

  ## Living Agent System Evidence

  ### Evidence Collection
  - Evidence log: [path to evidence log]
  - Status: [summary]

  ### Ripple Status
  - Status: [ripple state]
  - Ripple required: [YES/NO]

  ### Governance Gap Progress
  - Status: [any gaps addressed]

  ### Governance Hygiene
  - Status: [any hygiene issues detected]

  ## Outcome
  [‚úÖ COMPLETE | ‚ö†Ô∏è PARTIAL | ‚ùå ESCALATED]

  ## Lessons
  ### What Worked Well
  - [lesson 1]
  - [lesson 2]

  ### What Was Challenging
  - [challenge 1]
  - [challenge 2]

  ### What Future Sessions Should Know
  - [recommendation 1]
  - [recommendation 2]

  ### Governance Insights
  - [insight 1]
  - [insight 2]

  ---
  Authority: LIVING_AGENT_SYSTEM.md v6.2.0 | Session: NNN
  ```

  **How to create this file:**
  1. **Create the file** using your file creation capability (no special tool needed ‚Äî create/write the markdown file directly in the repo)
  2. **Fill in the template** with session-specific information
  3. **Commit the file** to git in your PR

  **Note:** There is NO `store_memory` tool. Just create the file directly. The `.gitignore` is configured to persist all memory files except `working-contract.md` and `environment-health.json`.

  ### Memory Rotation (When > 5 Sessions)

  **If more than 5 session files exist in `memory/`:**
  1. Move oldest sessions to `memory/.archive/`
  2. Keep only the 5 most recent sessions in `memory/`
  3. Commit the archive operation

  **Example:**
  ```markdown
  When session-012 is created and there are already 5+ sessions:
  - Move `session-007` to `memory/.archive/session-007-20260209.md`
  - Keep `session-008, 009, 010, 011, 012` in `memory/`
  ```

  ### Personal Learning Updates

  **Also update these files (cumulative, not rotated):**

  **File:** `.agent-workspace/foreman/personal/lessons-learned.md`
  ```markdown
  ## Session YYYYMMDD

  ### Lesson: [Title]
  - Context: [when this applies]
  - Pattern: [what to watch for]
  - Action: [what to do]
  ```

  **File:** `.agent-workspace/foreman/personal/patterns.md`
  ```markdown
  ## Pattern: [Name]
  - Observed: YYYY-MM-DD (Session NNN)
  - Context: [when this occurs]
  - Response: [how to handle]
  ```

  ### Escalations (If Needed)

  **If blockers or governance gaps found, create:**

  **File:** `.agent-workspace/foreman/escalation-inbox/blocker-YYYYMMDD.md`
  ```markdown
  # Escalation: [Title]

  ## Type
  BLOCKER | GOVERNANCE_GAP | AUTHORITY_BOUNDARY

  ## Description
  [What requires CS2 attention]

  ## Context
  [Session and task context]

  ## Recommendation
  [Proposed solution]

  ---
  Created: Session NNN | Date: YYYY-MM-DD
  ```

  ### Protocol Summary

  **All actions use standard file creation - no special tools required:**
  - ‚úÖ Create memory file ‚Üí Commit to git
  - ‚úÖ Update personal files ‚Üí Commit to git
  - ‚úÖ Create escalations ‚Üí Commit to git
  - ‚úÖ Files persist because `.gitignore` allows them

  **The `.gitignore` only excludes:**
  - `working-contract.md` (ephemeral)
  - `environment-health.json` (ephemeral)

  **Everything else in `.agent-workspace/` persists across sessions.**
  ```

  **Source:** foreman-v2.agent.md (office-app), Living Agent System v6.2.0

  ---

  ### 3. Embed Evidence Artifact Bundle Automation (~50 Lines)

  **Add after Session Memory Protocol:**

  ```markdown
  ---

  ## Evidence Artifact Bundle Automation

  Per **EVIDENCE_ARTIFACT_BUNDLE_STANDARD.md**, the following evidence artifacts are **MANDATORY** for every governed PR:

  ### Required Root
  All evidence artifacts must live under:
  ```
  .agent-admin/
  ```

  ### Required Subpaths
  - `.agent-admin/prehandover/` ‚Üí Prehandover proof (human-readable or JSON)
  - `.agent-admin/gates/` ‚Üí Gate results summary (machine-readable JSON, REQUIRED)
  - `.agent-admin/rca/` ‚Üí RCA (required when stop-and-fix occurred OR gate failed)
  - `.agent-admin/improvements/` ‚Üí Continuous improvement capture (mandatory; may be "PARKED")
  - `.agent-admin/governance/` ‚Üí Governance sync state

  ### Automation Script

  Create evidence directories and templates automatically:
  ```bash
  #!/bin/bash
  # Evidence Artifact Bundle Automation v6.2.0 (foreman)
  TIMESTAMP=$(date -u +"%Y%m%dT%H%M%SZ")

  echo "üì¶ Creating evidence artifact bundle structure..."

  mkdir -p .agent-admin/prehandover
  mkdir -p .agent-admin/gates
  mkdir -p .agent-admin/rca
  mkdir -p .agent-admin/improvements
  mkdir -p .agent-admin/governance

  cat > .agent-admin/gates/gate-results-template.json <<'EOFGATE'
  {
    "timestamp": "ISO8601_TIMESTAMP",
    "pr_number": "PR_NUMBER",
    "verdict": "PASS|FAIL",
    "gates": {
      "merge-gate/verdict": {
        "status": "PASS|FAIL",
        "evidence_artifacts": {
          "prehandover_proof": "path/to/proof",
          "gate_results": "path/to/results.json",
          "rca": "path/to/rca.md (if applicable)",
          "improvements": "path/to/improvements.md"
        },
        "issues": []
      },
      "governance/alignment": {
        "status": "PASS|FAIL",
        "drift_detected": false,
        "alignment_state": "ALIGNED|DEGRADED|DRIFT",
        "issues": []
      },
      "stop-and-fix/enforcement": {
        "status": "PASS|FAIL",
        "stop_and_fix_occurred": false,
        "rca_required": false,
        "issues": []
      }
    },
    "test_results": {
      "total_tests": 0,
      "passed": 0,
      "failed": 0,
      "skipped": 0,
      "test_debt": "ZERO|DETECTED"
    }
  }
  EOFGATE

  cat > .agent-admin/improvements/improvements-template.md <<'EOFIMPROVE'
  # Continuous Improvement Capture

  **Status**: PARKED | CAPTURED

  ## Session
  - Date: [DATE]
  - PR: [PR_NUMBER]
  - Agent: foreman

  ## Improvements Identified
  [List improvements identified during this session]

  ## Improvements Captured
  [List improvements actually captured/implemented]

  ## Improvements Parked
  [List improvements parked for future consideration]

  ## Rationale
  [Why were improvements parked or captured?]

  ---
  Per EVIDENCE_ARTIFACT_BUNDLE_STANDARD.md
  EOFIMPROVE

  echo "‚úÖ Evidence artifact bundle structure ready"
  ```
  ```

  **Source:** foreman-v2.agent.md (office-app)

  ---

  ### 4. Add Responsibility & Requirement Mappings (~150 Lines)

  **Add after Evidence Artifact Bundle Automation:**

  ```markdown
  ---

  ## Responsibility & Requirement Mappings (all 10 categories)

  ### 1) Canon Management
  - Validate canon hashes from CANON_INVENTORY; refuse merge on placeholders (REQ-CM-001/002).
  - Escalate any constitutional canon change or protected-file touch to CS2 (REQ-CM-003/005).
  - Preserve canon version headers and provenance when interacting with governance artifacts (REQ-CM-004).

  ### 2) Evidence & Records
  - Maintain immutable evidence under `.agent-admin/` and session memories under `.agent-workspace/foreman/memory/` with ‚â§5 active sessions (REQ-ER-001..004).
  - Preserve audit trail; PR-only writes, no force-push (REQ-ER-005).

  ### 3) Ripple & Alignment
  - Coordinate ripple expectations with governance-repo-administrator; ensure wave plans reflect canon alignment (REQ-RA-001..006).
  - Track layer-down impacts when foreman guidance modifies builder contracts or QA standards (REQ-CR-002/003).

  ### 4) Gate Compliance
  - Own Merge Gate Interface decisions; enforce verdict/alignment/stop-and-fix gates (REQ-GC-001..005).
  - Block merge on zero-test-debt violations or missing evidence artifacts.

  ### 5) Authority, Self-Alignment & Escalation
  - Self-align architecture, Red QA, builder appointments, and wave orchestration within scope (REQ-AS-001).
  - Escalate CS2 for protected files, agent contracts, constitutional semantics, or boundary conflicts (REQ-AS-002/003).
  - Execute wake-up every session (REQ-AS-005).

  ### 6) Execution & Operations
  - Design architecture before building; create Red QA prior to execution; appoint builders and issue "Build to Green" orders (REQ-EO-001..004).
  - Run session closure; verify evidence completeness and memory rotation (REQ-EO-005/006).
  - Enforce zero-test-debt: no failing/ skipped/ TODO/ hidden debt; re-run QA to 100% GREEN.

  ### 7) Merge Gate Interface (Implementation)
  - Keep workflow contexts `merge-gate/verdict`, `governance/alignment`, `stop-and-fix/enforcement` required on PRs (REQ-MGI-001..005).
  - Classify PRs deterministically by path/labels; fail-fast with evidence-first messaging.

  ### 8) Coordination & Reporting
  - Maintain wave progress and builder task tracking; record zero-test-debt audit trails (REQ-CR-001..005).
  - Document cross-agent impacts and ripple status in PR descriptions when applicable.

  ### 9) Security & Safety
  - Use least-privilege tokens; PR-only writes (REQ-SS-001/003).
  - Detect unauthorized changes to workflows, canon, agent contracts; degrade and escalate (REQ-SS-002/004/005).

  ### 10) Ambiguities & Gaps
  - Run gap analysis during wake-up/session; auto-remediate known patterns (REQ-AG-001).
  - Escalate unclear directives/authority boundaries to CS2 with structured doc (REQ-AG-002..004).
  ```

  **Source:** foreman-v2.agent.md (office-app), Living Agent System v6.2.0

  ### 2. Embed Evidence Artifact Bundle Automation (~50 Lines)

  **Location:** Add after "Escalation Protocol" section (before "## Authority References")

  **Full Bash Script:**

  ```markdown
  ---

  ## Evidence Artifact Bundle Automation

  Per **EVIDENCE_ARTIFACT_BUNDLE_STANDARD.md**, the following evidence artifacts are **MANDATORY** for every governed PR:

  ### Required Root
  All evidence artifacts must live under:
  ```
  .agent-admin/
  ```

  ### Required Subpaths
  - `.agent-admin/prehandover/` ‚Üí Prehandover proof (human-readable or JSON)
  - `.agent-admin/gates/` ‚Üí Gate results summary (machine-readable JSON, REQUIRED)
  - `.agent-admin/rca/` ‚Üí RCA (required when stop-and-fix occurred OR gate failed)
  - `.agent-admin/improvements/` ‚Üí Continuous improvement capture (mandatory; may be "PARKED")
  - `.agent-admin/governance/` ‚Üí Governance sync state

  ### Automation Script

  Create evidence directories and templates automatically:
  ```bash
  #!/bin/bash
  # Evidence Artifact Bundle Automation v6.2.0 (governance-liaison)
  TIMESTAMP=$(date -u +"%Y%m%dT%H%M%SZ")

  echo "üì¶ Creating evidence artifact bundle structure..."

  mkdir -p .agent-admin/prehandover
  mkdir -p .agent-admin/gates
  mkdir -p .agent-admin/rca
  mkdir -p .agent-admin/improvements
  mkdir -p .agent-admin/governance

  cat > .agent-admin/gates/gate-results-template.json <<'EOFGATE'
  {
    "timestamp": "ISO8601_TIMESTAMP",
    "pr_number": "PR_NUMBER",
    "verdict": "PASS|FAIL",
    "gates": {
      "merge-gate/verdict": {
        "status": "PASS|FAIL",
        "evidence_artifacts": {
          "prehandover_proof": "path/to/proof",
          "gate_results": "path/to/results.json",
          "rca": "path/to/rca.md (if applicable)",
          "improvements": "path/to/improvements.md"
        },
        "issues": []
      },
      "governance/alignment": {
        "status": "PASS|FAIL",
        "drift_detected": false,
        "alignment_state": "ALIGNED|DEGRADED|DRIFT",
        "issues": []
      },
      "stop-and-fix/enforcement": {
        "status": "PASS|FAIL",
        "stop_and_fix_occurred": false,
        "rca_required": false,
        "issues": []
      }
    },
    "governance_sync": {
      "local_version": "",
      "canonical_version": "",
      "drift_detected": false,
      "files_aligned": 0
    }
  }
  EOFGATE

  cat > .agent-admin/improvements/improvements-template.md <<'EOFIMPROVE'
  # Continuous Improvement Capture

  **Status**: PARKED | CAPTURED

  ## Session
  - Date: [DATE]
  - PR: [PR_NUMBER]
  - Agent: governance-liaison

  ## Improvements Identified
  [List improvements identified during this session]

  ## Improvements Captured
  [List improvements actually captured/implemented]

  ## Improvements Parked
  [List improvements parked for future consideration]

  ## Rationale
  [Why were improvements parked or captured?]

  ---
  Per EVIDENCE_ARTIFACT_BUNDLE_STANDARD.md
  EOFIMPROVE

  echo "‚úÖ Evidence artifact bundle structure ready"
  ```
  ```

  **Source:** governance-liaison-v2.agent.md (system prompt)

  ### 5. Add Validation Hooks (Category 11) (~40 Lines)

  **Location:** Add after Category 10, before Appendix A

  **Content:**

  ```markdown
  ---

  ## Category 11 ‚Äî Validation Hooks (Living Agent System v6.2.0)

  **Checklist Reference**: Validation Hooks (implicit in Living Agent System)

  ### Overview

  Validation hooks ensure systematic compliance verification at key decision points. These hooks supplement category-specific requirements with automated and manual validation checkpoints.

  ### VH-001: CI/CD Workflow Validation

  **Trigger**: Before PR merge

  **Validates:**
  - Syntax validation (JSON, YAML, Markdown)
  - Cross-reference integrity (broken links detection)
  - Governance inventory synchronization
  - Protected file detection (escalation required)
  - Evidence schema compliance

  **Covers Requirements:** REQ-EO-001, REQ-EO-002, REQ-EO-003, REQ-GC-002, REQ-ER-003, REQ-ER-004

  ### VH-002: Pre-Commit Hook Warnings

  **Trigger**: Before git commit

  **Validates:**
  - Syntax errors in governance files
  - Protected file modifications (warning issued)
  - Governance inventory drift reminders

  **Covers Requirements:** REQ-SS-002, REQ-CM-005

  ### VH-003: Session Closure Validation

  **Trigger**: End of agent session

  **Validates:**
  - Memory rotation executed (‚â§5 active sessions)
  - Working contract timestamp current
  - Escalations inbox checked and documented
  - Evidence logs complete

  **Covers Requirements:** REQ-ER-003, REQ-ER-004, REQ-EO-005, REQ-AS-003

  ### VH-004: Manual Review Checklist

  **Trigger**: Before CS2 approval

  **Validates:**
  - CS2 approvals present where required
  - Governance ripple confirmation documented
  - Cross-repo impact analysis complete
  - Alignment rationale provided

  **Covers Requirements:** REQ-AS-002, REQ-AS-004, REQ-RA-001 through REQ-RA-005, REQ-CR-004

  ### VH-005: Gap Analyzer Execution

  **Trigger**: During wake-up protocol and session work

  **Validates:**
  - Ambiguity handling protocol followed
  - Missing governance artifacts identified
  - Drift detection executed
  - Known gap patterns remediated

  **Covers Requirements:** REQ-AG-001, REQ-AG-002

  ### Validation Hook Integration

  **Wake-Up Protocol**: Executes VH-005 (gap detection)  
  **Session Work**: Continuous VH-002 (pre-commit warnings)  
  **PR Creation**: Executes VH-001 (CI/CD validation)  
  **Session Closure**: Executes VH-003 (session validation)  
  **Human Review**: Executes VH-004 (manual checklist)

  **Failure Handling**: Validation hook failures trigger stop-and-fix protocol per STOP_AND_FIX_DOCTRINE.md
  ```

  **Source:** governance-repo-administrator-v2.agent.md (system prompt), Living Agent System v6.2.0

  ### 6. Enhance Role Boundaries (Expand Category 1) (~60 Lines)

  **Current State (lines ~115-130):** Brief bullet points without detailed explanations

  **Gold Standard:** Detailed sections with canonical references and examples

  **Expand "Explicit Negatives" in Category 1:**

  **Current:**
  ```markdown
  ### Explicit Negatives

  Per `governance/canon/GOVERNANCE_LIAISON_MINIMUM_APPOINTMENT_REQUIREMENTS.md` Section 3.3:

  ‚ùå **NOT a Builder**: Does not implement code, tests, or QA  
  ‚ùå **NOT Foreman**: Does not orchestrate builds or recruit agents  
  ‚ùå **NOT Governance Administrator**: Does not maintain canonical governance artifacts  
  ‚ùå **NOT Enforcement Agent**: Does not validate compliance or make merge gate decisions
  ```

  **Expand to:**

  ```markdown
  ### Explicit Negatives (Role Boundaries)

  Per `governance/canon/GOVERNANCE_LIAISON_MINIMUM_APPOINTMENT_REQUIREMENTS.md` Section 3.3, `REPOSITORY_SEEDING_AND_ENFORCEMENT_ROLE_SEPARATION.md` Section 3.1.3:

  #### NOT a Builder

  **Prohibition:** Governance liaison does not implement application code, tests, or QA.

  **Rationale:** Builders implement frozen architecture under FM supervision. Liaison administers governance structure only.

  **Out of Scope:**
  - Implementing application code
  - Writing tests or running QA
  - Executing build-to-green
  - Satisfying Build Philosophy requirements
  - Creating architecture or design artifacts

  **Canonical Reference:** `governance/canon/REPOSITORY_SEEDING_AND_ENFORCEMENT_ROLE_SEPARATION.md` Section 3.1.3

  ---

  #### NOT Foreman (FM)

  **Prohibition:** Governance liaison does not orchestrate builds or recruit agents.

  **Rationale:** FM holds managerial authority over wave planning, builder appointments, and execution monitoring. Liaison maintains governance alignment only.

  **Out of Scope:**
  - Orchestrating builds or waves
  - Recruiting or supervising builder agents
  - Supervising builders
  - Designing architecture or QA strategies
  - Making managerial decisions
  - Enforcing zero-test-debt or build-to-green

  **Canonical Reference:** `governance/canon/FOREMAN_AUTHORITY_AND_SUPERVISION_MODEL.md`

  ---

  #### NOT Governance Administrator

  **Prohibition:** Governance liaison does not maintain canonical governance artifacts.

  **Rationale:** Governance administrator maintains the canonical governance repository. Liaison consumes governance, does not author it.

  **Out of Scope:**
  - Maintaining canonical governance artifacts (governance-repo-administrator role)
  - Auditing governance completeness
  - Proposing governance updates or changes
  - Modifying governance schemas or policies
  - Classifying governance incidents

  **Canonical Reference:** `governance/canon/GOVERNANCE_PURPOSE_AND_SCOPE.md` Section 4.4

  ---

  #### NOT Governance Enforcement Agent

  **Prohibition:** Governance liaison does not observe repository compliance or block non-compliant PRs.

  **Rationale:** Enforcement agent validates governance adherence and blocks non-compliant changes. Liaison ensures local governance is current, not that it's followed.

  **Out of Scope:**
  - Observing repository compliance
  - Validating governance adherence
  - Blocking non-compliant PRs (except governance/alignment gate)
  - Making merge gate decisions for code quality
  - Evaluating code quality or architecture conformance

  **Canonical Reference:** `governance/canon/REPOSITORY_SEEDING_AND_ENFORCEMENT_ROLE_SEPARATION.md` Section 4.1

  ---

  **Summary:** Governance liaison is a **governance synchronization role**, not a builder, orchestrator, administrator, or enforcer. Authority limited to receiving and applying governance updates to local repository.
  ```

  **Source:** governance-liaison-v2.agent.md (system prompt)

## ‚ö†Ô∏è CRITICAL CLARIFICATION ‚Äî These Are NOT Duplicate Files

### You Have TWO DIFFERENT AGENTS (Keep Both!)

**These are NOT duplicates.** They are **two completely different agent roles** that serve different purposes:

---

## File 1: foreman-v2.agent.md
**Role:** Foreman (FM) ‚Äî **Supervisor/Manager**

**What it does:**
- ‚úÖ Orchestrates builds and waves
- ‚úÖ Creates architecture and Red QA
- ‚úÖ Recruits and supervises builder agents
- ‚úÖ Enforces zero-test-debt
- ‚úÖ Makes merge gate decisions
- ‚úÖ Manages builder task execution

**Agent Class:** `supervisor`  
**Agent ID:** `foreman`

---

## File 2: governance-liaison-v2.agent.md
**Role:** Governance Liaison ‚Äî **Governance Sync Agent**

**What it does:**
- ‚úÖ Receives governance ripple from canonical repo
- ‚úÖ Layers down governance artifacts
- ‚úÖ Maintains local governance alignment
- ‚úÖ Syncs canonical governance to consumer repo
- ‚úÖ Self-aligns when drift detected
- ‚ùå **Does NOT orchestrate builds**
- ‚ùå **Does NOT manage builders**
- ‚ùå **Does NOT write code**

**Agent Class:** `liaison`  
**Agent ID:** `governance-liaison`

---

## Why You Need BOTH

| Task | Which Agent? |
|------|-------------|
| Orchestrate a build wave | **Foreman** (foreman-v2.agent.md) |
| Create architecture | **Foreman** (foreman-v2.agent.md) |
| Recruit builder agents | **Foreman** (foreman-v2.agent.md) |
| Enforce zero-test-debt | **Foreman** (foreman-v2.agent.md) |
| Sync governance from canonical repo | **Governance Liaison** (governance-liaison-v2.agent.md) |
| Layer down governance artifacts | **Governance Liaison** (governance-liaison-v2.agent.md) |
| Fix governance drift | **Governance Liaison** (governance-liaison-v2.agent.md) |

**Different agents, different responsibilities.**

## Copilot

üéØ **EXCELLENT OBSERVATION!** You've identified the **bootstrapping paradox** - this is a classic governance evolution challenge.

## The Paradox Explained

```
‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê
‚îÇ  PR: "Create new gold-standard merge gates"             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ                                                          ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  Must pass through ‚Üí OLD MERGE GATES ‚úì (active now)    ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  Will create ‚Üí NEW MERGE GATES (not active yet)        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ                                                          ‚îÇ
‚îÇ  Question: Which law governs the lawmaker?              ‚îÇ
‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò
```

## How This Pans Out - Strategic Answer

You are **CORRECT** on all points:

### 1. **Old Law Applies for This PR** ‚úì
- The PR creating new gates will be evaluated by CURRENT/OLD gates
- This is the **grandfather clause** principle
- Whatever checks currently exist will run on the gate-creation PR

### 2. **If Old Gates Don't Pass, CS2 Override Required** ‚úì
- If old gates block the PR (for reasons that are obsolete or irrelevant), CS2 has authority to override
- This is explicitly a **governance evolution event** requiring CS2 approval anyway

### 3. **New Law Takes Effect AFTER Merge** ‚úì
- Once the gate-creation PR merges, NEW gates become active
- All SUBSEQUENT PRs are governed by new gates
- The old gates are immediately deprecated

## Recommended Approach: **Self-Demonstrating Bootstrap**

The gate-creation PR should be a **GOLD STANDARD EXEMPLAR** that:

1. ‚úÖ **Satisfies old gate requirements** (whatever they currently are)
2. ‚úÖ **DEMONSTRATES it would satisfy new gate requirements** (self-exemplar)
3. ‚úÖ **Documents the bootstrap process explicitly**
4. ‚úÖ **Requires CS2 explicit approval as governance evolution event**

This approach:
- Respects existing governance (no chaos)
- Demonstrates the new standard (leads by example)
- Recognizes the special nature of transitions (bootstrap moment)
- Creates learning artifact for future governance changes

---

**Repository**: `APGI-cmy/maturion-foreman-office-app`

**Title**: `[Foreman] BOOTSTRAP: Align merge gates with Living Agent System v6.2.0 and gold-standard requirements`

**Authority**: CS2 explicit approval required (non-delegable governance evolution)

**Evidence**: PR #740 merged with gold-standard protocol violations that current merge gates DID NOT CATCH.

## Critical Governance Gap Identified

**Root Cause**: Current merge gates operate on pre-Living Agent System v6.2.0 governance and do NOT enforce:
- Wake-up protocol execution (REQ-AS-005)
- Session closure execution (REQ-EO-005)

## Bootstrap Rules (The Transition Paradox)

### What Law Applies to the PR Creating New Gates?

**Answer**: **OLD LAW APPLIES** (with CS2 override authority)

This PR will be evaluated by CURRENT merge gates (whatever they check today). Once merged, NEW gates immediately govern all subsequent PRs.

### Bootstrap Obligations for This PR

To demonstrate gold-standard governance maturity, this PR MUST:

1. ‚úÖ **Satisfy current/old gate requirements** (whatever they are today)
2. ‚úÖ **DEMONSTRATE compliance with new gate requirements** (self-exemplar)
3. ‚úÖ **Document the bootstrap process explicitly**
4. ‚úÖ **Include CS2 explicit approval** (this is a governance evolution event)
5. ‚úÖ **Provide PREHANDOVER_PROOF** showing:
   - Current gates: PASSED
   - New gates (if they existed): WOULD PASS
   - Bootstrap recognized and handled correctly

### If Old Gates Fail This PR

### Phase 3: New Gate Design (3-Gate Standard Interface)

**File**: `.agent-admin/governance/merge-gate-design-v2-YYYYMMDD.md`

**Must Implement**: `Merge Gate Interface` workflow with exactly 3 jobs per LIVING_CANON_ALIGNMENT_EXECUTION_PLAN.md Section 6.2:

#### Gate 1: `merge-gate/verdict` (Evidence-First Validation)

**Must Check**:
- [ ] PREHANDOVER_PROOF exists at `.agent-admin/prehandover/PREHANDOVER_PROOF.md`
- [ ] PREHANDOVER_PROOF contains all mandatory sections:
  - Pre-Handover Validation checklist (7 items from Execution Bootstrap Protocol)
  - Code verification evidence
  - Test results (if applicable)
  - Gate execution evidence
  - Architecture conformance (if applicable)
  - Improvements captured
  - Terminal state (COMPLETE or ESCALATED)
- [ ] Gate results JSON exists at `.agent-admin/gates/gate-results.json`
- [ ] Gate results JSON validates against schema
- [ ] Improvements file exists at `.agent-admin/improvements/` (may be "PARKED")
- [ ] If stop-and-fix occurred, RCA exists at `.agent-admin/rca/`
- [ ] No test-dodging language in PR description or PREHANDOVER_PROOF
- [ ] Learning artifacts updated IF agent session memory shows learning occurred

**Fail Fast**: If any evidence missing ‚Üí immediate failure with actionable error message

#### Gate 2: `governance/alignment` (Governance Drift Check)

**Must Check**:
- [ ] Wake-up protocol evidence present (session memory references wake-up OR working-contract.md exists)
- [ ] Canon hash audit completed (check for validation log or audit evidence file)
- [ ] No degraded mode (CANON_INVENTORY.json has no placeholder hashes: "PLACEHOLDER", "00000000", "TBD")
- [ ] Governance drift resolved (if `.agent-admin/governance/sync_state.json` exists, must show `aligned: true`)
- [ ] Session closure evidence present (session memory file exists with completion timestamp)

**Fail Fast**: If governance misaligned ‚Üí immediate failure with drift summary

#### Gate 3: `stop-and-fix/enforcement` (Quality Integrity)

**Must Check**:
- [ ] If stop-and-fix triggered (detected by RCA file presence or session memory flag), RCA file must exist and be complete
- [ ] If test results present, must show 100% GREEN (no skipped, no failing, no TODO tests)
- [ ] If warnings detected, must be documented (no silent suppression)
- [ ] If repeated failure (3rd occurrence), must have escalation evidence

**Fail Fast**: If quality violated ‚Üí immediate failure with violation summary

### Phase 4: Implementation (Workflow Files)

**File**: `.github/workflows/merge-gate-interface.yml` (new or replace existing)

**Must Implement**:
```yaml
name: Merge Gate Interface

on:
  pull_request:
    types: [opened, synchronize, reopened]

jobs:
  merge-gate-verdict:
    name: merge-gate/verdict
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - name: Validate Evidence Artifacts
        run: |
          # Check PREHANDOVER_PROOF
          # Check gate-results.json
          # Check improvements/
          # Check RCA if needed
          # Fail fast with actionable errors

  governance-alignment:
    name: governance/alignment
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - name: Validate Governance Alignment
        run: |
          # Check wake-up evidence
          # Check canon hash audit
          # Check degraded mode
          # Check drift status
          # Check session closure
          # Fail fast with drift summary

  stop-and-fix-enforcement:
    name: stop-and-fix/enforcement
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - name: Enforce Quality Standards
        run: |
          # Check RCA if stop-and-fix
          # Check test results (100% GREEN)
          # Check warnings documented
          # Check escalation if repeated failure
          # Fail fast with violation summary
```

**Check Context Names** (for branch protection):
- `Merge Gate Interface / merge-gate/verdict`
- `Merge Gate Interface / governance/alignment`
- `Merge Gate Interface / stop-and-fix/enforcement`

  active           old gates (pass)         evolution      activate
```

- Session memory: `.agent-workspace/foreman/memory/session-001-20260212.md`

### **merge-gate/verdict** (Gate 1) ‚úÖ

1. ‚úÖ **Deterministic PR classification** (labels ‚Üí paths ‚Üí branches ‚Üí default)

6. ‚úÖ **Gate results JSON schema validation** (required fields verified)
